Introduction
Dental caries, or tooth decay, is a common chronic disease

Chunk 134:
that can cause pain, suffering, and diminished quality of life
throughout ones lifespan.1 Left untreated, tooth decay can
progress and lead to infection, tooth loss, and more complex

Chunk 135:
and expensive treatments. Untreated tooth decay can affect
essential aspects of daily living, including eating, speaking, and
performing at home, school, or work.1 Children with poor oral

Chunk 136:
health miss more school and receive lower grades than those
with better oral health, while adults lose more school or work
hours for urgent, unplanned dental visits.24

Chunk 137:
